        <script type="text/javascript">
            var currency = {"formatPattern":"$###,###.##","fractionalSize":2,"groupingSeparator":",","groupingSize":3,"decimalSeparator":"."};
            var showSmallCents = true;
            var isBrandedFarePointsEnabled = false
            function formatSmallCents(price)
            {
                if(showSmallCents)
                {
                    var pat = RegExp( "\\" + currency.decimalSeparator + "[\\d]*(?=$|\\s)");

                    if( pat.test( price ))

    require(['jquery', 'xsellDX', 'handlebars'], function( $, DestinationExperienceUDP, Handlebars ){

        var activityUrl =  "/lx/api/search-xsell?vbpEnabled=true&startDate=04-06-21&endDate=04-13-21&regionId=179995&c=bf57df3a-caae-443b-92fc-9b32e5e6448a&otla=BAQ&dtla=CUN&rotla=CUN&rdtla=BAQ&carrier=AV&hotelId=980531&categoryId=2&sortByRank=true&locale=en_US&imageHeight=116&imageWidth=206&hopSortEnabled=true&hotelLatLong=21.100221,-86.76712&pricingServiceEnabled=true&lxAllDestinationActivityEnabled=true";
        var transportUrl =  "/ground-transfers/api/search-xsell?vbpEnabled=true&startDate=04-06-21&endDate=04-13-21&regionId=179995&c=bf57df3a-caae-443b-92fc-9b32e5e6448a&otla=BAQ&dtla=CUN&rotla=CUN&rdtla=BAQ&carrier=AV&hotelId=980531&categoryId=1&locale=en_US&oneClickGTUDPEnabled=true&pricingServiceEnabled=true";
        window.isLxIntegrationWithMultiItemDomainEnabled = false;
        window.isLxIntegrationWithUPPEnabled = window.isLxIntegrationWithMultiItemDomainEnabled && false;
        window.isLxUisPrimeLoggingEnabled = true;

            var moduleName = "UDPLXACTIVIIESV2";

            var ssIdRegX = /c=[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}/;
            var transKey =  transportUrl.replace(ssIdRegX, "");
            var activityKey =  activityUrl.replace(ssIdRegX, "");

            if (window.isLxIntegrationWithMultiItemDomainEnabled) {
                var flightPiidRegX = /flightPIID=[a-zA-Z0-9-~.]*&/;
                transKey =  transportUrl.replace(flightPiidRegX, "");
                activityKey =  activityUrl.replace(flightPiidRegX, "");
            }

            var dxSelection = typeof(g_dxSelection) !== "undefined"? g_dxSelection: null;
            DestinationExperienceUDP.create(
                    "/lx/api/search-xsell?vbpEnabled=true&startDate=04-06-21&endDate=04-13-21&regionId=179995&c=bf57df3a-caae-443b-92fc-9b32e5e6448a&otla=BAQ&dtla=CUN&rotla=CUN&rdtla=BAQ&carrier=AV&hotelId=980531&categoryId=2&sortByRank=true&locale=en_US&imageHeight=116&imageWidth=206&hopSortEnabled=true&hotelLatLong=21.100221,-86.76712&pricingServiceEnabled=true&lxAllDestinationActivityEnabled=true",
                    "/ground-transfers/api/search-xsell?vbpEnabled=true&startDate=04-06-21&endDate=04-13-21&regionId=179995&c=bf57df3a-caae-443b-92fc-9b32e5e6448a&otla=BAQ&dtla=CUN&rotla=CUN&rdtla=BAQ&carrier=AV&hotelId=980531&categoryId=1&locale=en_US&oneClickGTUDPEnabled=true&pricingServiceEnabled=true",
                    "Add to trip",
                    "Update",
                    dxSelection,
                    edxCallback);
            Handlebars.registerHelper('if_eq', function(arg1, arg2, opts) {
                if(arg1 == arg2)
                    return opts.fn(this);
                else
                    return opts.inverse(this);
            });
            Handlebars.registerHelper('gte', function(context, n, options) {
                return DestinationExperienceUDP.gte(context,n,options,this);
            });

            function xsellSearchCall(url,key)
            {
                if (sessionStorage && sessionStorage.getItem(key))
                {
                    logWithCondition();
                    document.getElementById("xsellParentContainer").setAttribute("class", "show");
                    DestinationExperienceUDP.flightUrgencyData();
                    return;
                }
                try
                {
                    var httpObj=new XMLHttpRequest();

                    httpObj.onreadystatechange=function()
                    {
                        xsellResponse(httpObj,key);
                    }
                    httpObj.open("GET",url,true);
                    httpObj.send();
                }
                catch(err)
                {
                    //do nothing
                }
            }

            function xsellResponse(httpObj,key)
            {
            if (httpObj.readyState==4 && httpObj.status==200)
                {
                    var data = JSON.parse(httpObj.responseText);
                    var list = {};
                    if(window.isLxIntegrationWithMultiItemDomainEnabled) {
                        list = $.map(data.dxProducts, function(value, index) {
                            return [value];
                        });
                    }
                    else {
                        list = data ? data.productList : data;
                    }

                    if ($.isArray(list) && list.length > 0) {
                        document.getElementById("xsellParentContainer").setAttribute("class", "show");
                        if (sessionStorage)
                        {
                            sessionStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(list));
                        }
                        logWithCondition();
                    }

                    if(data && data.searchFailureMessage === 'search results are unavailable')
                    {
                        if ( key.indexOf("&categoryId=1") > -1 || key.indexOf("lxCategoryId=1") > -1 )
                        {
                            DestinationExperienceUDP.updateOmnitureTaggingForXSellResultCount("PKG|GT:", 0);
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            DestinationExperienceUDP.updateOmnitureTaggingForXSellResultCount("PKG|LX:", 0);
                        }
                    }

                    if($.isArray(list))
                    {
                        if ( key.indexOf("&categoryId=1") > -1 || key.indexOf("lxCategoryId=1") > -1)
                        {
                            DestinationExperienceUDP.updateOmnitureTaggingForXSellResultCount("PKG|GT:", list.length);
                            DestinationExperienceUDP.flightUrgencyData();
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            DestinationExperienceUDP.updateOmnitureTaggingForXSellResultCount("PKG|LX:", list.length);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        //this tells if the experiment is already logged by GX call when this function is called second time with LX. thus needs to be higher scope then the funciton.
        var isLogged = false;
        function logWithCondition(){
            var isPKGResponsive;
                isPKGResponsive = true;
            if (isPKGResponsive && isLogged === false){
                if(window.dctk && dctk.enabled) {
                    dctk.onReady(function () {
                        dctk.addExperiments("11439." + 1);
                    });
                }
                isLogged = true;
            }
        }

            var osid ="bf57df3a-caae-443b-92fc-9b32e5e6448a";

            function edxCallback( data, dxSelection, notify, isGTAvailable)
            {
                renderGtBanner(dxSelection, isGTAvailable);

                if( data.prcLineItem && tripSummary)
                {
                    tripSummary.updateDxDetails(dxSelection);
                    tripSummary.updateTripSummary( data.prcLineItem );
                    if (typeof creditCardPromoUpdate === 'function') { creditCardPromoUpdate( data.prcLineItem);}
                    delete dxSelection.tsModel;
                }
                var dxSelectionJSON = JSON.stringify(dxSelection);

                $("#id-udp-book-now-form input[name='dxSelection'],#id-udp-save-to-itin-link input[name='dxSelection']").val(dxSelectionJSON);
                if( notify )
                {
                    $.ajax({
                        url : "/DX-Update-Context?c=" + osid,
                        type : "POST",
                        dataType: "json",
                        data : "dxSelection=" + dxSelectionJSON,
                        cache : false,
                        success : function(resp)
                        {
                            emptyPriceChangeMessage();
                            if(resp)
                            {
                                //TODO: Add backButton support when Vasu gets done wit dxSelection retrieve
                                if(backButtonSupport && typeof resp  === "string")
                                {
                                    backButtonSupport.register( resp );
                                    osid = resp;
                                }
                                //update session id in nav-tool-language href (if exists) - so we don't lose dxSelection
                                var changeLangUrl = $("#nav-tool-language").attr("href");
                                if( changeLangUrl)
                                {
                                    ssIdRegX = /c=[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}/;

                                    var match = changeLangUrl.match(ssIdRegX);
                                    if(match.length == 1)
                                    {
                                        changeLangUrl = changeLangUrl.replace( match[0], "c=" + resp  );
                                        $("#nav-tool-language").attr("href", changeLangUrl);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }
            }

        function emptyPriceChangeMessage(){
            var $priceChangeMessageEl = $('#priceChangeMessage');
            if ($priceChangeMessageEl.length)
            {
                $priceChangeMessageEl.html("");
            }
        }
        function renderGtBanner(dxSelection, isGTAvailable)
        {
            var showGtBanner = isGTAvailable;
            var model = dxSelection.tsModel;
            for (var i=0; i < model.length; i++)
            {
                if (model[i].Type === "Transp")
                {
                    showGtBanner = false;
                    break;
                }
            }
                DestinationExperienceUDP.updateTripSummaryGtBanner(showGtBanner);
        }

        function removeDxItem(error,dxItemId)
        {
            $(error).parent(".dxMessage").remove();
            DestinationExperienceUDP.removeDxItem(dxItemId);
            if($("#dxErrorMessages .dxMessage").length == 0)
                $("#dxErrorMessages").remove();
            return false;
        }

        window.removeDxItem = function(error, dxItemId)
        {
            removeDxItem(error, dxItemId);
        }

    });
